clare my determination as set out in the Schedule a ppended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of  Land No. 28 of Block 07, contained 
in the Cadastral Map No. 510600, situated in the Vil lage of Kalalpitiya within the Grama Niladhari Divi sion of No. 343 - Kalalpitiya in 
the Divisional Secretary's Division of Attanagalla,  in the District of Gampaha, in the Province of Wes tern, referred to in Notice No. 
51/0374 calling for claims to land parcels which wa s duly published in the Gazette No. 1743/18 of 02nd  February, 2012 in terms of 
Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998.

clare my determination as set out in the Schedule a ppended hereto in regard to the  title to parcel of  Land Nos. 30, 53, 56, 92, 94, 102, 
123, 184, 185 and 322 of Block 03, contained in the Cadastral Map No. 510636, situated in the Village of Welagedara within the Grama 
Niladhari Division of No. 353 - Welagedara in the D ivisional Secretary's Division of Attanagalla, in t he District of Gampaha, in the 
Province of Western, referred to in Notice No. 51/0 994 calling for claims to land parcels which was du ly published in the Gazette No. 
2043/41 of 01st November, 2017 in terms of Section 12 of the Registration of Title Act, No.21 of 1998.
